### [215] [Safety Margins of Inverse Optimal ISSf Controllers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.26397)
*Ziliang Lyu,Yiguang Hong,Lihua Xie,Miroslav Krstic*

Main category: eess.SY

TL;DR: 本文研究了非线性系统在逆最优输入到状态安全（ISSf）控制器下的增益裕度，揭示了标准控制器在不同场景下的增益裕度，并提出了一种改进方法以提高对增益变化的鲁棒性，确保全局渐近稳定性和在存在扰动时的鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在理解和量化逆最优ISSf控制器在增益变化下的安全性和稳定性，因为现有的控制器可能对扰动敏感，且其增益裕度特性尚未被充分探究，尤其是在不同安全边界条件下的表现。

Method: 首先建立了逆ISSf-BF定理的逆定理，揭示了ISSf的可实现性、逆最优性与Hamilton-Jacobi-Isaacs方程可解性之间的等价性。然后，针对总控制律u=u0+u*，推导了一系列安全裕度结果。最后，提出了一种以增加控制代价为代价的增益裕度改进方法，以增强控制器对增益变化的鲁棒性。

Result: 研究发现，在无扰动情况下，标准逆最优安全控制器具有一定程度的增益裕度：当f(x)安全但u0不安全时，增益可减半；当f(x)不安全但u0安全时，增益可任意增加；当f(x)和u0都不安全时，增益裕度为[1/2,inf)。然而，这些控制器的安全集在控制增益变化下是局部渐近稳定的，表明对大的有界扰动敏感。提出的改进方法使逆最优安全控制继承了[1/2,inf)的标准增益裕度，无需预先知道f(x)或u0在安全边界上的行为，同时确保了所得安全集的全局渐近稳定性。在存在扰动的情况下，该改进方法使逆最优ISSf控制器对增益变化具有相同的[1/2,inf)增益裕度。

Conclusion: 逆最优ISSf控制器在特定条件下具有固有的增益裕度，但其安全性可能对大的扰动敏感。通过提出的增益裕度改进方法，可以显著增强逆最优ISSf控制器对增益变化的鲁棒性，实现全局渐近稳定性，并在存在扰动时保持良好的增益裕度，从而提高了控制系统的整体可靠性和安全性。

Abstract: We investigate the gain margin of a general nonlinear system under an inverse
optimal input-to-state safe (ISSf) controller of the form u=u0(x)+u*(x,u0),
where u0 is the nominal control and u* is the inverse optimal safety filter
that minimally modifies the nominal controller's unsafe actions over the
infinite horizon. By first establishing a converse ISSf-BF theorem, we reveal
the equivalence among the achievability of ISSf by feedback, the achievability
of inverse optimality, and the solvability of a Hamilton-Jacobi-Isaacs equation
associated with the inverse optimal ISSf gain assignment. Then we develop a
collection of safety margin results on the overall control u=u0+u*. In the
absence of disturbances, we find that standard inverse optimal safe controllers
have a certain degree of gain margin. Specifically, when f(x) acts safely but
u0 acts unsafely, the gain can be decreased by up to half; and when f(x) acts
unsafely, we establish that, if u0 acts safely, the gain can be increased
arbitrarily, whereas if u0 acts unsafely, the control recovers the full gain
margin [1/2,inf). It is shown, however, that under control gain variation, the
safe set of these controllers is locally asymptotically stable, which implies
that their safety is sensitive to large but bounded disturbances. To make
inverse optimal ISSf controllers robust to gain variation, we propose a gain
margin improvement approach at the expense of an increased control effort. This
improvement allows the inverse optimal safe control to inherit the standard
gain margin of [1/2,inf) without requiring prior knowledge of whether f(x) or
u0 acts safely on the safety boundary, while simultaneously ensuring global
asymptotic stability of the resulting safe set. In the presence of
disturbances, this improvement idea renders inverse optimal ISSf controllers
robust to gain variations with the same gain margin of [1/2,inf).

</details>


### [216] [Pareto-Optimal Sampling and Resource Allocation for Timely Communication in Shared-Spectrum Low-Altitude Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.26708)
*Bowen Li,Jiping Luo,Themistoklis Charalambous,Nikolaos Pappas*

Main category: eess.SY

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种图基算法，用于在共享频谱中为低空无人机实现严格的数据新鲜度，通过在无人机能耗和地面信道资源占用之间找到帕累托最优平衡，显著降低了资源利用率或能耗。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在共享频谱中，为低空无人机（UAV）保证严格的数据新鲜度，需要在无人机自身能耗和地面信道资源占用之间进行关键权衡。核心挑战是在满足空中数据新鲜度的同时，找到这些成本之间的帕累托最优平衡。

Method: 利用预测性信道模型和无人机轨迹，将问题建模为一个长期规划视域上的双目标帕累托优化问题，以联合优化空中流量的采样时机以及功率和频谱分配。通过揭示帕累托前沿的单调性，将双目标问题转化为多个单目标问题。然后，提出了一种新的图基算法，并证明其能够以低复杂度（与规划时域线性相关，与资源块预算近似二次相关）找到完整的帕累托最优解集。

Result: 所提出的算法能够找到完整的帕累托最优解集，且复杂度较低。数值比较表明，该方法不仅满足了严格的实时性要求，而且与基准方法相比，实现了资源块利用率降低六倍或能耗节省6 dB。

Conclusion: 本研究开发了一种高效的图基算法，能够为在共享频谱中运行的无人机找到数据新鲜度保证的帕累托最优解决方案，有效平衡能耗和频谱资源占用，并在资源利用或能效方面实现了显著提升。

Abstract: Guaranteeing stringent data freshness for low-altitude unmanned aerial
vehicles (UAVs) in shared spectrum forces a critical trade-off between two
operational costs: the UAV's own energy consumption and the occupation of
terrestrial channel resources. The core challenge is to satisfy the aerial data
freshness while finding a Pareto-optimal balance between these costs.
Leveraging predictive channel models and predictive UAV trajectories, we
formulate a bi-objective Pareto optimization problem over a long-term planning
horizon to jointly optimize the sampling timing for aerial traffic and the
power and spectrum allocation for fair coexistence. However, the problem's
non-convex, mixed-integer nature renders classical methods incapable of fully
characterizing the complete Pareto frontier. Notably, we show monotonicity
properties of the frontier, building on which we transform the bi-objective
problem into several single-objective problems. We then propose a new
graph-based algorithm and prove that it can find the complete set of Pareto
optima with low complexity, linear in the horizon and near-quadratic in the
resource block (RB) budget. Numerical comparisons show that our approach meets
the stringent timeliness requirement and achieves a six-fold reduction in RB
utilization or a 6 dB energy saving compared to benchmarks.

### [217] [Time-Optimal Model Predictive Control for Linear Systems with Multiplicative Uncertainties](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.26712)
*Renato Quartullo,Andrea Garulli,Mirko Leomanni*

Main category: eess.SY

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种针对乘性不确定性线性离散时间系统的时最优模型预测控制（MPC）方案，通过矩阵zonotope近似不确定性传播，实现计算可处理性，并通过离线计算显著降低在线负担。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用时最优模型预测控制（MPC）方案；使用基于矩阵zonotope的边界算子近似集合值误差系统动力学，以处理不确定性传播；通过自适应终端约束机制确保递归可行性和有限时间收敛；所有必要的边界集均可离线计算，以减少在线计算负担。

Result: 不确定性传播计算可处理；确保了递归可行性和有限时间收敛；由于离线计算，显著降低了在线计算负担；通过卫星轨道交会演习的数值案例研究证明了方法的有效性。

Conclusion: 所提出的时最优MPC方案能够有效地控制具有乘性不确定性的线性离散时间系统，通过矩阵zonotope和离线计算实现计算效率，并保证系统的稳定性和收敛性。

Abstract: This paper presents a time-optimal Model Predictive Control (MPC) scheme for
linear discrete-time systems subject to multiplicative uncertainties
represented by interval matrices. To render the uncertainty propagation
computationally tractable, the set-valued error system dynamics are
approximated using a matrix-zonotope-based bounding operator. Recursive
feasibility and finite-time convergence are ensured through an adaptive
terminal constraint mechanism. A key advantage of the proposed approach is that
all the necessary bounding sets can be computed offline, substantially reducing
the online computational burden. The effectiveness of the method is illustrated
via a numerical case study on an orbital rendezvous maneuver between two
satellites.

### [219] [BitSemCom: A Bit-Level Semantic Communication Framework with Learnable Probabilistic Mapping](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.26225)
*Haoshuo Zhang,Yufei Bo,Jianhua Mo,Meixia Tao*

Main category: eess.IV

TL;DR: BitSemCom提出了一种新的比特级语义通信框架，通过可学习的比特映射器实现真正的比特级联合源信道编码，解决了现有系统与数字通信不兼容、缺乏端到端比特级方法的问题，并展现出优越的性能和鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大多数现有语义通信系统采用模拟调制，与现代数字通信系统不兼容。虽然已有一些数字传输方法，但仍缺乏一种兼容任意调制格式、对信道噪声鲁棒且无量化误差的端到端比特级方法。

Method: 本文提出了BitSemCom，一个新颖的比特级语义通信框架，实现真正的比特级联合源信道编码（JSCC）。具体地，引入了一个模块化的可学习比特映射器，利用Gumbel-Softmax技巧，在连续语义特征和离散比特之间建立概率映射，从而实现可微分的比特生成。

Result: 在图像传输仿真中，BitSemCom与传统分离源信道编码（SSCC）方案相比，实现了具有竞争力的性能和卓越的鲁棒性。它优于基于深度学习且采用均匀1比特量化的JSCC方案，验证了可学习比特映射器的有效性。此外，比特映射器仅增加0.42%的参数和0.09%的计算复杂度。

Conclusion: BitSemCom通过其比特级联合源信道编码和高效的可学习比特映射器，为实际语义通信提供了一个轻量级且实用的解决方案，在性能和鲁棒性方面均表现出色。

Abstract: Most existing semantic communication systems employ analog modulation, which
is incompatible with modern digital communication systems. Although several
digital transmission approaches have been proposed to address this issue, an
end-to-end bit-level method that is compatible with arbitrary modulation
formats, robust to channel noise, and free from quantization errors remains
lacking. To this end, we propose BitSemCom, a novel bit-level semantic
communication framework that realizes true joint source-channel coding (JSCC)
at the bit level. Specifically, we introduce a modular learnable bit mapper
that establishes a probabilistic mapping between continuous semantic features
and discrete bits, utilizing the Gumbel-Softmax trick to enable differentiable
bit generation. Simulation results on image transmission demonstrate that
BitSemCom achieves both competitive performance and superior robustness
compared to traditional separate source-channel coding (SSCC) schemes, and
outperforms deep learning based JSCC with uniform 1-bit quantization,
validating the effectiveness of the learnable bit mapper. Despite these
improvements, the bit mapper adds only 0.42% parameters and 0.09% computational
complexity, making BitSemCom a lightweight and practical solution for
real-world semantic communication.

### [220] [Functional Connectome Fingerprinting Using Convolutional and Dictionary Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.26120)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 该研究提出了一种结合卷积自编码器和稀疏字典学习的框架。自编码器用于捕捉共享的功能连接模式，并将个体特异性特征分离到残差FC矩阵中。随后，使用稀疏编码技术分析这些残差矩阵，以识别独特的个体特征。

Result: 在Human Connectome Project数据集上进行测试，该方法比基线组平均FC模型取得了10%的性能提升。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明，整合深度学习和稀疏编码技术在可扩展和鲁棒的功能连接指纹识别方面具有巨大潜力，有助于推动个性化神经科学应用和生物标志物开发。

and behavior through individual neural patterns. Functional connectivity (FC),
which quantifies statistical relationships between brain regions, has emerged
as a key metric for studying individual variability and developing biomarkers
for personalized medicine in neurological and psychiatric disorders. The
concept of subject fingerprinting, introduced by Finn et al. (2015), leverages
neural connectivity variability to identify individuals based on their unique
patterns. While traditional FC methods perform well on small datasets, machine
learning techniques are more effective with larger datasets, isolating
individual-specific features and maximizing inter-subject differences. In this
study, we propose a framework combining convolutional autoencoders and sparse
dictionary learning to enhance fingerprint accuracy. Autoencoders capture
shared connectivity patterns while isolating subject-specific features in
residual FC matrices, which are analyzed using sparse coding to identify
distinctive features. Tested on the Human Connectome Project dataset, this
approach achieved a 10% improvement over baseline group-averaged FC models. Our
results highlight the potential of integrating deep learning and sparse coding
techniques for scalable and robust functional connectome fingerprinting,
advancing personalized neuroscience applications and biomarker development.

</details>


### [221] [SPG-CDENet: Spatial Prior-Guided Cross Dual Encoder Network for Multi-Organ Segmentation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.26390)
*Xizhi Tian,Changjun Zhou,Yulin. Yang*

Main category: eess.IV

TL;DR: 本文提出SPG-CDENet，一种用于多器官分割的两阶段深度学习范式。它通过空间先验网络生成粗略ROI指导，并结合交叉双编码器网络（包含全局/局部编码器、对称交叉注意力模块和基于流的解码器）来处理器官大小和形状的巨大变异，显著提高了分割精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多器官分割在计算机辅助诊断中至关重要，但器官大小和形状的巨大变异性严重挑战了现有深度学习方法在此任务中的有效性。

Method: 本文提出SPG-CDENet，一个两阶段分割范式。第一阶段，空间先验网络生成粗略的ROI定位图作为空间指导；第二阶段，交叉双编码器网络包含：1) 全局编码器捕获整体图像特征；2) 局部编码器关注先验网络提供的区域特征；3) 对称交叉注意力模块在编码器各层间融合和细化特征；4) 基于流的解码器将最终编码层的高级语义特征直接传播到所有解码器层，以最大化特征保留和利用。

Result: 在两个公共数据集上进行的广泛定性和定量实验表明，SPG-CDENet相比现有分割方法具有卓越的性能。此外，消融研究进一步验证了所提出模块在提高分割精度方面的有效性。

Conclusion: SPG-CDENet通过其新颖的两阶段架构（空间先验指导和交叉双编码器网络），成功解决了多器官分割中器官变异性带来的挑战，实现了更高的分割精度。

Abstract: Multi-organ segmentation is a critical task in computer-aided diagnosis.
While recent deep learning methods have achieved remarkable success in image
segmentation, huge variations in organ size and shape challenge their
effectiveness in multi-organ segmentation. To address these challenges, we
propose a Spatial Prior-Guided Cross Dual Encoder Network (SPG-CDENet), a novel
two-stage segmentation paradigm designed to improve multi-organ segmentation
accuracy. Our SPG-CDENet consists of two key components: a spatial prior
network and a cross dual encoder network. The prior network generates coarse
localization maps that delineate the approximate ROI, serving as spatial
guidance for the dual encoder network. The cross dual encoder network comprises
four essential components: a global encoder, a local encoder, a symmetric
cross-attention module, and a flow-based decoder. The global encoder captures
global semantic features from the entire image, while the local encoder focuses
on features from the prior network. To enhance the interaction between the
global and local encoders, a symmetric cross-attention module is proposed
across all layers of the encoders to fuse and refine features. Furthermore, the
flow-based decoder directly propagates high-level semantic features from the
final encoder layer to all decoder layers, maximizing feature preservation and
utilization. Extensive qualitative and quantitative experiments on two public
datasets demonstrate the superior performance of SPG-CDENet compared to
existing segmentation methods. Furthermore, ablation studies further validate
the effectiveness of the proposed modules in improving segmentation accuracy.

</details>


### [222] [Comparative Analysis of Deep Learning Models for Olive Tree Crown and Shadow Segmentation Towards Biovolume Estimation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.26573)
*Wondimagegn Abebe Demissie,Stefano Roccella,Rudy Rossetto,Antonio Minnocci,Andrea Vannini,Luca Sebastiani*

Main category: eess.IV

TL;DR: 本研究比较了U-Net、YOLOv11m-seg和Mask R-CNN三种深度学习模型，用于从无人机图像中分割橄榄树冠及其阴影，并通过结合冠投影面积和阴影高度估算橄榄树的生物体积，以支持精准农业。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 精准农业中橄榄树生物体积估算对于产量预测和资源管理至关重要，特别是在受气候变化影响严重的地中海地区。

Method: 研究采用超高分辨率无人机图像数据集，包含人工标注的树冠和阴影掩模。在此基础上，比较了U-Net、YOLOv11m-seg和Mask R-CNN三种深度学习模型进行分割。随后，利用太阳几何学原理，结合树冠投影面积和阴影推导的高度来估算单棵树的生物体积。

Result: Mask R-CNN在整体准确性上表现最佳（F1 = 0.86；mIoU = 0.72），而YOLOv11m-seg提供了最快的处理速度（每张图像0.12秒）。估算的生物体积范围约为4到24立方米，反映了树木之间明显的结构差异。

Conclusion: 当生物体积估算精度至关重要时，Mask R-CNN是首选；当速度是关键的大面积部署场景中，YOLOv11m-seg更具优势；U-Net则是一个轻量级、高灵敏度的选择。该框架能够实现准确、可扩展的果园监测，并可通过集成DEM或DSM以及现场校准进一步强化，以支持操作决策。

Abstract: Olive tree biovolume estimation is a key task in precision agriculture,
supporting yield prediction and resource management, especially in
Mediterranean regions severely impacted by climate-induced stress. This study
presents a comparative analysis of three deep learning models U-Net,
YOLOv11m-seg, and Mask RCNN for segmenting olive tree crowns and their shadows
in ultra-high resolution UAV imagery. The UAV dataset, acquired over
Vicopisano, Italy, includes manually annotated crown and shadow masks. Building
on these annotations, the methodology emphasizes spatial feature extraction and
robust segmentation; per-tree biovolume is then estimated by combining crown
projected area with shadow-derived height using solar geometry. In testing,
Mask R-CNN achieved the best overall accuracy (F1 = 0.86; mIoU = 0.72), while
YOLOv11m-seg provided the fastest throughput (0.12 second per image). The
estimated biovolumes spanned from approximately 4 to 24 cubic meters,
reflecting clear structural differences among trees. These results indicate
Mask R-CNN is preferable when biovolume accuracy is paramount, whereas
YOLOv11m-seg suits large-area deployments where speed is critical; U-Net
remains a lightweight, high-sensitivity option. The framework enables accurate,
scalable orchard monitoring and can be further strengthened with DEM or DSM
integration and field calibration for operational decision support.

### [223] [SAMRI: Segment Anything Model for MRI](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.26635)
*Zhao Wang,Wei Dai,Thuy Thanh Dao,Steffen Bollmann,Hongfu Sun,Craig Engstrom,Shekhar S. Chandra*

Main category: eess.IV

TL;DR: SAMRI是一个针对MRI图像分割的专用SAM模型，通过简单地微调其掩码解码器，显著减少了训练时间和参数，并在各种MRI分割任务中实现了最先进的准确性和强大的泛化能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: MRI图像的精确分割对临床决策至关重要，但手动分割劳动密集。基于CNN的方法在MRI图像对比度、强度不均匀性和协议多样性方面泛化性差。现有的Transformer-based SAM模型虽然在自然图像上表现出色，但其MRI适应性往往忽视了MRI特有的挑战。

Method: 本文提出了SAMRI，一个MRI专用的SAM模型。通过两阶段策略，仅微调SAM的掩码解码器，而不是重新训练整个模型。该模型在涵盖全身器官和病理的110万张标注MR切片上进行训练和验证。

Result: SAMRI在训练时间上减少了94%，可训练参数减少了96%（与全模型再训练相比）。在各种MRI分割任务中，SAMRI实现了0.87的平均Dice分数，在解剖区域上达到了最先进的准确性，并对未见过的结构（特别是小型和临床重要结构）表现出鲁棒的泛化能力。

Conclusion: 通过简单地微调SAM的掩码解码器，SAM模型可以有效地适应MRI图像分割任务，从而实现高效、高精度且泛化能力强的MRI分割，解决了MRI特有的挑战。

Abstract: Accurate magnetic resonance imaging (MRI) segmentation is crucial for
clinical decision-making, but remains labor-intensive when performed manually.
Convolutional neural network (CNN)-based methods can be accurate and efficient,
but often generalize poorly to MRI's variable contrast, intensity
inhomogeneity, and protocols. Although the transformer-based Segment Anything
Model (SAM) has demonstrated remarkable generalizability in natural images,
existing adaptations often treat MRI as another imaging modality, overlooking
these modality-specific challenges. We present SAMRI, an MRI-specialized SAM
trained and validated on 1.1 million labeled MR slices spanning whole-body
organs and pathologies. We demonstrate that SAM can be effectively adapted to
MRI by simply fine-tuning its mask decoder using a two-stage strategy, reducing
training time by 94% and trainable parameters by 96% versus full-model
retraining. Across diverse MRI segmentation tasks, SAMRI achieves a mean Dice
of 0.87, delivering state-of-the-art accuracy across anatomical regions and
robust generalization on unseen structures, particularly small and clinically
important structures.

### [224] [BRIQA: Balanced Reweighting in Image Quality Assessment of Pediatric Brain MRI](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.26661)
*Alya Almsouti,Ainur Khamitova,Darya Taratynova,Mohammad Yaqub*

Main category: eess.IV

TL;DR: 该研究提出BRIQA，一种用于儿科脑部MRI图像伪影严重程度自动评估的解决方案，通过梯度损失重加权和旋转批处理解决类别不平衡问题，显著提高了分类性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 儿科脑部MRI图像中伪影严重程度的评估对于诊断准确性至关重要，尤其是在低场系统中。手动质量评估耗时且主观，因此需要鲁棒的自动化解决方案。

Method: 本文提出了BRIQA（图像质量评估中的平衡重加权）方法，旨在解决伪影严重程度级别中的类别不平衡问题。BRIQA采用基于梯度的损失重加权来动态调整每个类别的贡献，并使用旋转批处理方案以确保欠代表类别获得一致的曝光。研究还强调了架构多样性的重要性，因为没有单一架构在所有伪影类型上表现最佳。

Result: 旋转批处理配置与交叉熵损失结合使用时，通过促进平衡学习，提高了各项指标的性能。BRIQA将平均宏观F1分数从0.659提高到0.706，并在噪声（0.430）、拉链（0.098）、定位（0.097）、对比度（0.217）、运动（0.022）和条带（0.012）伪影严重程度分类方面取得了显著提升。

Conclusion: BRIQA通过有效解决类别不平衡问题，显著提高了儿科脑部MRI伪影严重程度分类的性能。该方法强调了平衡学习策略和架构多样性对于鲁棒自动化评估的重要性。

Abstract: Assessing the severity of artifacts in pediatric brain Magnetic Resonance
Imaging (MRI) is critical for diagnostic accuracy, especially in low-field
systems where the signal-to-noise ratio is reduced. Manual quality assessment
is time-consuming and subjective, motivating the need for robust automated
solutions. In this work, we propose BRIQA (Balanced Reweighting in Image
Quality Assessment), which addresses class imbalance in artifact severity
levels. BRIQA uses gradient-based loss reweighting to dynamically adjust
per-class contributions and employs a rotating batching scheme to ensure
consistent exposure to underrepresented classes. Through experiments, no single
architecture performs best across all artifact types, emphasizing the
importance of architectural diversity. The rotating batching configuration
improves performance across metrics by promoting balanced learning when
combined with cross-entropy loss. BRIQA improves average macro F1 score from
0.659 to 0.706, with notable gains in Noise (0.430), Zipper (0.098),
Positioning (0.097), Contrast (0.217), Motion (0.022), and Banding (0.012)
artifact severity classification. The code is available at
https://github.com/BioMedIA-MBZUAI/BRIQA.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: ProstNFound+系统结合了一个医学基础模型、适配器微调技术和一个定制的提示编码器，该编码器能够嵌入前列腺癌特异性的临床生物标志物。该模型能生成癌症热图和临床显著性前列腺癌的风险评分。模型首先在多中心回顾性数据上进行训练，然后在一个新的临床站点获取的前瞻性数据上进行评估，并与标准临床评分协议（PRI-MUS和PI-RADS）进行比较。

Conclusion: 研究结果突显了ProstNFound+在临床部署方面的巨大潜力，为专家驱动的诊断协议提供了一种可扩展且可解释的替代方案。

Abstract: Purpose: Medical foundation models (FMs) offer a path to build
high-performance diagnostic systems. However, their application to prostate
cancer (PCa) detection from micro-ultrasound ({\mu}US) remains untested in
clinical settings. We present ProstNFound+, an adaptation of FMs for PCa
detection from {\mu}US, along with its first prospective validation. Methods:
ProstNFound+ incorporates a medical FM, adapter tuning, and a custom prompt
encoder that embeds PCa-specific clinical biomarkers. The model generates a

prospective data, with no performance degradation compared to retrospective
evaluation. It aligns closely with clinical scores and produces interpretable
heatmaps consistent with biopsy-confirmed lesions. Conclusion: The results
highlight its potential for clinical deployment, offering a scalable and
interpretable alternative to expert-driven protocols.

### [226] [MORE: Multi-Organ Medical Image REconstruction Dataset](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.26759)
*Shaokai Wu,Yapan Guo,Yanbiao Ji,Jing Tong,Yuxiang Lu,Mei Li,Suizhi Huang,Yue Ding,Hongtao Lu*

TL;DR: 本文介绍了MORE数据集，一个包含9种解剖结构和15种病变类型的多器官CT重建数据集，旨在解决深度学习CT重建模型泛化能力差的问题，并提出了一个性能优于现有方法的基线解决方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前的深度学习CT重建方法通常局限于特定解剖结构和数据集，导致对未见过的解剖结构和病变泛化能力不足。

Method: 研究人员构建了多器官医学图像重建（MORE）数据集，该数据集包含9种不同的解剖结构和15种病变类型的CT扫描。该数据集用于模型训练和泛化能力评估。此外，他们还建立了一个强大的基线解决方案。

Result: MORE数据集有助于提高模型的泛化能力；基于优化的方法对未见过的解剖结构表现出更强的鲁棒性；所提出的基线解决方案在这些挑战性条件下优于现有方法。

Conclusion: 一个全面的异构数据集能显著提升CT重建模型的泛化能力，且基于优化的方法在处理未知解剖结构时表现出更好的鲁棒性，为未来的CT重建研究提供了重要资源和方向。

Abstract: CT reconstruction provides radiologists with images for diagnosis and
treatment, yet current deep learning methods are typically limited to specific
anatomies and datasets, hindering generalization ability to unseen anatomies
and lesions. To address this, we introduce the Multi-Organ medical image

with 15 lesion types. This dataset serves two key purposes: (1) enabling robust
training of deep learning models on extensive, heterogeneous data, and (2)
facilitating rigorous evaluation of model generalization for CT reconstruction.
We further establish a strong baseline solution that outperforms prior
approaches under these challenging conditions. Our results demonstrate that:
(1) a comprehensive dataset helps improve the generalization capability of
models, and (2) optimization-based methods offer enhanced robustness for unseen
anatomies. The MORE dataset is freely accessible under CC-BY-NC 4.0 at our
